 Rise of Bhindranwale In the 70s, when the fire of separatism was spreading in Punjab, a seven-year-old innocent child in Chowk Mehta area of amritsar arrived in Damdami Mint to study Sikhism
 badi shiddat ke saath us bachche ne vahaan sikh dharm kii talim lenaa shuru kiya
